# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 07:39:38.937599

### Base Program

```py
def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def maximumElementAfterDecrementingAndRearranging(arr: List[int]) -> int:
    arr.sort()
    arr[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        arr[i] = min(arr[i], arr[i - 1] + 1)
    return arr[-1]


```
